				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.RCW_green_var_Muscovy
						value = 10
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = RCW_green_Muscovy_revolt
			}
			country_event = { id = rcw_g.0 days = 365 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = RUS_RCW_start_green NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_RCW_green_over }
				check_variable = { global.RCW_green_jule < 4 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { global.RCW_green_jule = 1 }
		}
	}
}

							militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
						is_locked = yes
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
						is_locked = yes
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes tag = HRB
							}
						}

					}
				}
				RUS = { set_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists }
			}
			RGR = { set_state_owner = 205 set_province_controller = 274 }
			205 = {
				set_state_flag = RCW_green_state_revolt

					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}

								}

							NOT = { has_war_with = RGR }
							#NOT = { has_completed_focus = IZH_third_way }
							NOT = { has_completed_focus = VLG_attraction_of_peasant_leaders }

								NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_attraction_of_peasant_leaders }
								has_global_flag = RCW_green_Russian_SFSR_revolt_b
							}
						}

							declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = annex_everything }
						}
					}
			}
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } RUS = { country_event = { id = rcw_g.4 days = 60 random = 960 } clr_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } }
	}

###Ливенское восстание###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_g.15
	title = rcw_g.15.t
	desc = rcw_g.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_rgr_village_revolution

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		always = no
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		has_government = communism
		has_idea = RUS_prodrazverstka_idea
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = RUS_prodnalog_idea
				has_country_flag = war_communism_abolished
			}
		}
		date > 1918.08.01
		controls_state = 222
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_g.15.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = RGR }
			}
				RGR = {
					add_ideas = {
						control_of_field_commanders_law
						RGR_urban_rural_antogonism
						RGR_power_decentralisation
						RGR_supply_bonus
					}
					remove_ideas = {
						RGR_consolidation_of_units_idea
						RGR_fraternizing_with_proletariat_idea
						RGR_red_banditry_idea
						RGR_councils_without_communists_idea
						RGR_working_peasantry_unions_idea
						RGR_uprisings_coordination_idea
						RGR_peasant_gatherings_idea
						RGR_associations_of_veterans_idea
						RGR_recruitment_officers_idea
						RGR_single_headquarters_idea
						RGR_peasant_army_idea
						RGR_punitive_forces_idea
						RGR_atamanshina_idea
						RGR_forest_brothers_idea
						RGR_deserters_collection_idea
						RGR_free_cossackship_idea
						RGR_cavalry_raiding_idea
						RGR_voluntary_mobilization_idea
					}
					load_focus_tree = { tree = Russia_Green_rebels keep_completed = no }
					set_politics = { ruling_party = radical_socialism elections_allowed = no }
					division_template = {
						name = "Pekhotnaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
						is_locked = yes
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }

								tag = PREV

								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes tag = HRB
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
				RUS = { set_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists }
			}
			RGR = { set_state_owner = 222 set_province_controller = 328 }
			222 = {
				set_state_flag = RCW_green_state_revolt
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								any_country = {
									is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
									has_war_with = PREV
								}
								is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_war_with = RGR }
							#NOT = { has_completed_focus = IZH_third_way }
							NOT = { has_completed_focus = VLG_attraction_of_peasant_leaders }
							OR = {
								NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_attraction_of_peasant_leaders }

							}

						}

###Акулевское восстание###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_g.20
	title = rcw_g.20.t
	desc = rcw_g.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_rgr_village_revolution

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		always = no
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		has_government = communism
		has_idea = RUS_prodrazverstka_idea
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = RUS_prodnalog_idea
				has_country_flag = war_communism_abolished
			}
		}
		date > 1921.01.19
		controls_state = 256
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_g.20.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = RGR }
			}
				RGR = {
					add_ideas = {
						control_of_field_commanders_law
						RGR_urban_rural_antogonism

					}

						RGR_consolidation_of_units_idea
						RGR_fraternizing_with_proletariat_idea
						RGR_red_banditry_idea
						RGR_councils_without_communists_idea
						RGR_working_peasantry_unions_idea
						RGR_uprisings_coordination_idea
						RGR_peasant_gatherings_idea
						RGR_associations_of_veterans_idea
						RGR_recruitment_officers_idea
						RGR_single_headquarters_idea
						RGR_peasant_army_idea
						RGR_punitive_forces_idea

						RGR_forest_brothers_idea
						RGR_deserters_collection_idea

							militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }

						}

					}
				}
				RUS = { set_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists }
			}
			RGR = { set_state_owner = 256 set_province_controller = 11356 }
			256 = {
				set_state_flag = RCW_green_state_revolt
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR

								NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_attraction_of_peasant_leaders }
								has_global_flag = RCW_green_Russian_SFSR_revolt_b
							}
						}
						RGR = {
							declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = annex_everything }
						}
					}
			}
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } RUS = { country_event = { id = rcw_g.4 days = 60 random = 960 } clr_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } }
	}

###Колесниковщина###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_g.25
	title = rcw_g.25.t
	desc = rcw_g.25.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_rgr_village_revolution

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		always = no
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		has_government = communism
		has_idea = RUS_prodrazverstka_idea
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = RUS_prodnalog_idea
				has_country_flag = war_communism_abolished
			}
		}
		date > 1920.07.14
		controls_state = 260
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_g.25.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = RGR }
			}
				RGR = {
					add_ideas = {
						control_of_field_commanders_law
						RGR_urban_rural_antogonism
						RGR_power_decentralisation
						RGR_supply_bonus
					}
					remove_ideas = {
						RGR_consolidation_of_units_idea
						RGR_fraternizing_with_proletariat_idea
						RGR_red_banditry_idea
						RGR_councils_without_communists_idea
						RGR_working_peasantry_unions_idea
						RGR_uprisings_coordination_idea
						RGR_peasant_gatherings_idea
						RGR_associations_of_veterans_idea
						RGR_recruitment_officers_idea
						RGR_single_headquarters_idea
						RGR_peasant_army_idea
						RGR_punitive_forces_idea
						RGR_atamanshina_idea
						RGR_forest_brothers_idea
						RGR_deserters_collection_idea
						RGR_free_cossackship_idea
						RGR_cavalry_raiding_idea
						RGR_voluntary_mobilization_idea
					}
					load_focus_tree = { tree = Russia_Green_rebels keep_completed = no }
					set_politics = { ruling_party = radical_socialism elections_allowed = no }
					division_template = {
						name = "Pekhotnaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
						is_locked = yes
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
						is_locked = yes
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes tag = HRB
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
				RUS = { set_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists }
			}
			RGR = { set_state_owner = 260 set_province_controller = 11412 }
			260 = {
				set_state_flag = RCW_green_state_revolt
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								any_country = {
									is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
									has_war_with = PREV
								}
								is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_war_with = RGR }
							#NOT = { has_completed_focus = IZH_third_way }
							NOT = { has_completed_focus = VLG_attraction_of_peasant_leaders }
							OR = {
								NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_attraction_of_peasant_leaders }
								has_global_flag = RCW_green_Russian_SFSR_revolt_b
							}
						}
						RGR = {
							declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = annex_everything }
						}
					}
			}
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } RUS = { country_event = { id = rcw_g.4 days = 60 random = 960 } clr_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } }
	}
}

		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } RUS = { country_event = { id = rcw_g.4 days = 60 random = 960 } clr_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } }
	}

###Чапанная война###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_g.30
	title = rcw_g.30.t
	desc = rcw_g.30.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_rgr_village_revolution

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		always = no
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		has_government = communism
		has_idea = RUS_prodrazverstka_idea
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = RUS_prodnalog_idea
				has_country_flag = war_communism_abolished
			}
		}
		date > 1919.03.03
		controls_state = 250
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_g.30.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = RGR }
			}
				RGR = {
					add_ideas = {
						control_of_field_commanders_law
						RGR_urban_rural_antogonism
						RGR_power_decentralisation
						RGR_supply_bonus
					}
					remove_ideas = {
						RGR_consolidation_of_units_idea
						RGR_fraternizing_with_proletariat_idea
						RGR_red_banditry_idea
						RGR_councils_without_communists_idea
						RGR_working_peasantry_unions_idea
						RGR_uprisings_coordination_idea
						RGR_peasant_gatherings_idea
						RGR_associations_of_veterans_idea
						RGR_recruitment_officers_idea
						RGR_single_headquarters_idea
						RGR_peasant_army_idea
						RGR_punitive_forces_idea
						RGR_atamanshina_idea
						RGR_forest_brothers_idea
						RGR_deserters_collection_idea
						RGR_free_cossackship_idea
						RGR_cavalry_raiding_idea
						RGR_voluntary_mobilization_idea
					}
					load_focus_tree = { tree = Russia_Green_rebels keep_completed = no }
					set_politics = { ruling_party = radical_socialism elections_allowed = no }
					division_template = {
						name = "Pekhotnaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
						is_locked = yes
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
						is_locked = yes
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes tag = HRB
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
				RUS = { set_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists }
			}
			RGR = { set_state_owner = 250 set_province_controller = 6275 }
			250 = {
				set_state_flag = RCW_green_state_revolt
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" division_template = \"Pekhotnaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = RGR
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								any_country = {
									is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
									has_war_with = PREV
								}
								is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_war_with = RGR }
							#NOT = { has_completed_focus = IZH_third_way }
							NOT = { has_completed_focus = VLG_attraction_of_peasant_leaders }
							OR = {
								NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_attraction_of_peasant_leaders }
								has_global_flag = RCW_green_Russian_SFSR_revolt_b
							}
						}
						RGR = {
							declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = annex_everything }
						}
					}
			}
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } RUS = { country_event = { id = rcw_g.4 days = 60 random = 960 } clr_country_flag = RGR_dont_exists } } }
	}
}

###Разруха таймер###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_g.32
	
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_devastation_fired }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "[?global.RUS_devastation]"
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_intervention_start
					has_global_flag = RUS_monarchy_Petrograd_commune_civil_war
					has_global_flag = RUS_Kornilov_civil_war
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 1.5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_state = { region = 132 NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = CONTROLLER } }
					any_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 132 } any_other_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 132 } has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_state = { region = 133 NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = CONTROLLER } }
					any_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 133 } any_other_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 133 } has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_state = { region = 306 NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = CONTROLLER } }
					any_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 306 } any_other_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 306 } has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_state = { OR = { region = 135 region = 302 } NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = CONTROLLER } }
					any_country = { any_controlled_state = { OR = { region = 135 region = 302 } } any_other_country = { any_controlled_state = { OR = { region = 135 region = 302 } } has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_state = { region = 301 NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = CONTROLLER } }
					any_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 301 } any_other_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 301 } has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_state = { region = 40 NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = CONTROLLER } }
					any_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 40 } any_other_country = { any_controlled_state = { region = 40 } has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_state = { OR = { region = 138 region = 308 region = 14 region = 151 } NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = CONTROLLER } }
					any_country = { any_controlled_state = { OR = { region = 138 region = 308 region = 14 region = 151 } } any_other_country = { any_controlled_state = { OR = { region = 138 region = 308 region = 14 region = 151 } } has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_state = { OR = { region = 148 region = 255 region = 149 region = 258 } NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = CONTROLLER } }
					any_country = { any_controlled_state = { OR = { region = 148 region = 255 region = 149 region = 258 } } any_other_country = { any_controlled_state = { OR = { region = 148 region = 255 region = 149 region = 258 } } has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_state = { OR = { region = 130 region = 303 } NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = CONTROLLER } }
					any_country = { any_controlled_state = { OR = { region = 130 region = 303 } } any_other_country = { any_controlled_state = { OR = { region = 130 region = 303 } } has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RGR
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 0.5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = { OR = { has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_loyal has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_disloyal } has_war = yes }
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_devastation value = 1.5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { global.RUS_devastation > 700 } #312  #270
			}
			set_global_flag = RUS_devastation_fired
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
					any_other_country = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes has_war_with = PREV }
					NOT = { tag = RGR }
				}
				country_event = rcw.102
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
					NOT = { any_other_country = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes has_war_with = PREV } }
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_devastation_leave_before
			}
			else = { random_country = { country_event = { id = rcw_g.32 days = 7 } } }
		}
	}
}

###Ишимский процесс###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_g.35
	title = rcw_g.35.t
	desc = rcw_g.35.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_rgr_village_revolution
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		has_government = communism
		OR = {
			has_idea = RUS_prodnalog_idea
			has_idea = RUS_prodrazverstka_idea
		}
		check_variable = { RCW_green_var_Russian_SFSR > 3 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_g.35.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.RCW_green_var_Russian_SFSR
			value = 3
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_to_variable = { left_faction_party_compositon = 0.05 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = left_fact_party_comp_plus_5
		check_overlap_of_party_composition = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_g.35.b
		trigger = { left_fact_party_is_ruling = no }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.07
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_political_power = -10
		add_to_variable = { left_faction_party_compositon = -0.05 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = left_fact_party_comp_minus_5
		check_overlap_of_party_composition = yes
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.RCW_green_var_Russian_SFSR
			value = 2
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_g.35.c
		trigger = { left_fact_party_is_ruling = no }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		add_political_power = -30
		if = {
			limit = { decist_fact_party_is_ruling = yes }
			add_to_variable = { decist_faction_party_compositon = -0.1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = decist_fact_party_comp_minus_10
			check_overlap_of_party_composition = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { center_fact_party_is_ruling = yes }
			add_to_variable = { center_faction_party_compositon = -0.1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = center_fact_party_comp_minus_10
			check_overlap_of_party_composition = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { moderate_fact_party_is_ruling = yes }
			add_to_variable = { moderate_faction_party_compositon = -0.1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = moderate_fact_party_comp_minus_10
			check_overlap_of_party_composition = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { right_fact_party_is_ruling = yes }
			add_to_variable = { right_faction_party_compositon = -0.1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = right_fact_party_comp_minus_10
			check_overlap_of_party_composition = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.RCW_green_var_Russian_SFSR
			value = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_g.39
	title = rcw_g.39.t
	desc = rcw_g.39.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_rgr_the_uprising_of_the_chieftains
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_g.39.a
		BKI = {
            every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = RGR
						is_controlled_by = RGR
					}
					OR = {
					    state = 566
					    state = 568
						state = 567
				    }
				}
				BKI = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			hidden_effect = { add_state_core = 566 add_state_core = 568 add_state_core = 567 }

            RGR = { retire_character = RGR_Nestor_Kalandarishvili }
			recruit_character = RGR_Nestor_Kalandarishvili
			retire_ideology_leader = communism
            hidden_effect = {
			    add_ideas = soviet_republic_gov_form
			    add_ideas = local_assembly_decisions_b_law
			    add_ideas = dominant_party_system_law
			    add_ideas = ideological_expansion_law
			    add_ideas = control_of_field_commanders_law
				add_ideas = unitary_gov_terr

			    add_ideas = lack_of_officers_2
			    add_ideas = CCA_no_money
			    add_ideas = RUS_weak_state_suppression_apparatus_1
			    add_ideas = RUS_damage_to_police_and_special_services
			    add_ideas = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_1
			    add_ideas = collapse_of_railway_systemss_2
				add_ideas = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_25
			}

			load_focus_tree = Tree_Red_Rebels

			custom_effect_tooltip = RGR_vosstanye_ataman_2_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = RGR_vosstanye_ataman_1_tt
            hidden_effect = {
			    division_template = {
				    name = "Krestyanskoe opolchenie"
				    regiments = {
					    militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					    militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					    militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				    }
				    is_locked = no
			    }
			    division_template = {
				    name = "Kavalerijskaya sotnya"
				    regiments = {
					    irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					    irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					    irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				    }
				    is_locked = no
			    }
			    every_state = {
				    create_unit = {
					    division = "name = \"Krestyanskoe opolchenie\" division_template = \"Krestyanskoe opolchenie\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 1"
					    owner = PREV
					    count = 3
				    }
				    create_unit = {
					    division = "name = \"Kavalerijskaya sotnya\" division_template = \"Kavalerijskaya sotnya\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 1"
					    owner = PREV
					    count = 1
				    }
			    }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = RGR
				type = annex_everything
			}
            every_country = {
				limit = { has_offensive_war_with = ROOT NOT = { has_war_with = BKI } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = BKI
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_defensive_war_with = ROOT NOT = { has_war_with = BKI } }
				BKI = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		BKI = { change_tag_from = RGR }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_g.39.b
		BKI = {
            every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = RGR
